Release 1.0 (Jul 23, 2010)
Incompatible changes
Â· Support for domains has been added. A domain is a collection of directives and roles that all describe objects belonging together, e.g. elements of a programming language. A
few builtin domains are provided:

Â· Python

Â· C

Â· C++

Â· JavaScript

Â· reStructuredText

Â· The old markup for defining and linking to C directives is now deprecated. It will not work anymore in future versions without activating the oldcmarkup extension; in Sphinx
1.0, it is activated by default.

Â· Removed support for old dependency versions; requirements are now:

Â· docutils >= 0.5

Â· Jinja2 >= 2.2

Â· Removed deprecated elements:

Â· exclude_dirs config value

Â· sphinx.builder module

Features added
Â· General:

Â· Added a ânitpickyâ mode that emits warnings for all missing references. It is activated by the sphinx-build -n command-line switch or the nitpicky config value.

Â· Added latexpdf target in quickstart Makefile.

Â· Markup:

Â· The menuselection and guilabel roles now support ampersand accelerators.

Â· New more compact doc field syntax is now recognized: :param type name: description.

Â· Added tab-width option to literalinclude directive.

Â· Added titlesonly option to toctree directive.

Â· Added the prepend and append options to the literalinclude directive.

Â· #284: All docinfo metadata is now put into the document metadata, not just the author.

Â· The ref role can now also reference tables by caption.

Â· The include directive now supports absolute paths, which are interpreted as relative to the source directory.

Â· In the Python domain, references like :func:‘.name‘ now look for matching names with any prefix if no direct match is found.

Â· Configuration:

Â· Added rst_prolog config value.

Â· Added html_secnumber_suffix config value to control section numbering format.

Â· Added html_compact_lists config value to control docutilsâ compact lists feature.

Â· The html_sidebars config value can now contain patterns as keys, and the values can be lists that explicitly select which sidebar templates should be rendered. That means
that the builtin sidebar contents can be included only selectively.

Â· html_static_path can now contain single file entries.

Â· The new universal config value exclude_patterns makes the old unused_docs, exclude_trees and exclude_dirnames obsolete.

Â· Added html_output_encoding config value.

Â· Added the latex_docclass config value and made the âtwosideâ documentclass option overridable by âonesideâ.

Â· Added the trim_doctest_flags config value, which is true by default.

Â· Added html_show_copyright config value.

Â· Added latex_show_pagerefs and latex_show_urls config values.

Â· The behavior of html_file_suffix changed slightly: the empty string now means âno suffixâ instead of âdefault suffixâ, use None for âdefault suffixâ.

Â· New builders:

Â· Added a builder for the Epub format.

Â· Added a builder for manual pages.

Â· Added a single-file HTML builder.

Â· HTML output:

Â· Inline roles now get a CSS class with their name, allowing styles to customize their appearance. Domain-specific roles get two classes, domain and domain-rolename.

Â· References now get the class internal if they are internal to the whole project, as opposed to internal to the current page.

Â· External references can be styled differently with the new externalrefs theme option for the default theme.

Â· In the default theme, the sidebar can experimentally now be made collapsible using the new collapsiblesidebar theme option.

Â· #129: Toctrees are now wrapped in a div tag with class toctree-wrapper in HTML output.

Â· The toctree callable in templates now has a maxdepth keyword argument to control the depth of the generated tree.

Â· The toctree callable in templates now accepts a titles_only keyword argument.

Â· Added htmltitle block in layout template.

Â· In the JavaScript search, allow searching for object names including the module name, like sys.argv.

Â· Added new theme haiku, inspired by the Haiku OS user guide.

Â· Added new theme nature.

Â· Added new theme agogo, created by Andi Albrecht.

Â· Added new theme scrolls, created by Armin Ronacher.

Â· #193: Added a visitedlinkcolor theme option to the default theme.

Â· #322: Improved responsiveness of the search page by loading the search index asynchronously.

Â· Extension API:

Â· Added html-collect-pages.

Â· Added needs_sphinx config value and require_sphinx() application API method.

Â· #200: Added add_stylesheet() application API method.

Â· Extensions:

Â· Added the viewcode extension.

Â· Added the extlinks extension.

Â· Added support for source ordering of members in autodoc, with autodoc_member_order = ’bysource’.

Â· Added autodoc_default_flags config value, which can be used to select default flags for all autodoc directives.

Â· Added a way for intersphinx to refer to named labels in other projects, and to specify the project you want to link to.

Â· #280: Autodoc can now document instance attributes assigned in __init__ methods.

Â· Many improvements and fixes to the autosummary extension, thanks to Pauli Virtanen.

Â· #309: The graphviz extension can now output SVG instead of PNG images, controlled by the graphviz_output_format config value.

Â· Added alt option to graphviz extension directives.

Â· Added exclude argument to autodoc.between().

Â· Translations:

Â· Added Croatian translation, thanks to Bojan MihelaÄ.

Â· Added Turkish translation, thanks to Firat Ozgul.

Â· Added Catalan translation, thanks to Pau FernÃ¡ndez.

Â· Added simplified Chinese translation.

Â· Added Danish translation, thanks to Hjorth Larsen.

Â· Added Lithuanian translation, thanks to Dalius Dobravolskas.

Â· Bugs fixed:

Â· #445: Fix links to result pages when using the search function of HTML built with the dirhtml builder.

Â· #444: In templates, properly re-escape values treated with the âstriptagsâ Jinja filter.

Previous versions
The changelog for versions before 1.0 can be found in the file CHANGES.old in the source distribution or at GitHub.
